buildFactoriesByType().release();\n   218→\n   219→    return *factories_by_type;\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  static bool& allowDuplicates() {\n   223→    static bool* allow_duplicates = new registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   231→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   232→    auto result =   240→    }\n   241→  }\n   242→\n   243→  /**\n   244→   * version is used for registering vendor specific factories that are versioned\n   245→   * independently of Envoy.\n   246→   */\n   247→  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   248→                              const envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion& version,\n   249→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   250→    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n   251→    if (!result.second) {\n   252→ If the factory is registered under multiple\n   264→   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   265→   */\n   266→  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   267→    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n   268→      auto it = factories().find(name);\n   269→      if (it != factories().end()) {\n   270→        it->second = nullptr;\n   271→        return true;\n   272→      }\n   273→      return false;\n   274→    };\n   275→\n   276→    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n   277→    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n   278→\n   279→    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n   280→    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n   281→      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n   282→        disable(deprecated_name);\n   283→      }\n   284→    }\n   285→\n   286→    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n   287→    return disable(canonicalName);\n   288→  }\n   289→\n   290→  /**\n   291→   * Gets a factory by name. 315→    const auto it = deprecatedFactoryNames().find(name);\n   316→    return (it == deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) ? name : it->second;\n   317→  }\n   318→\n   319→  /**\n   320→   * @return true This enforces correct use of the registration machinery.\n  template <class T, class Base> friend class RegisterFactory;\n  template <class Base> friend class InjectFactoryCategory;\n\n  static void registerCategory(const std::string& category, FactoryRegistryProxy* factory_names) {\n    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(category, factory_names));\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(result.second == true,\n                   fmt::format(\"Double registration for category: '{}'\", category));\n  }\n\n  static void deregisterCategoryForTest(const std::string& category) {\n    factories().erase(category);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(factories().find(category) == factories().end(),\n                   fmt::format(\"Deregistration for category '{}' failed\", category));\n  }\n};\n\n// Forward declaration of test class for friend declaration below.\ntemplate <typename T> class InjectFactory;\n\n/**\n * General registry for implementation factories. The registry is templated by the Base class that a\n * set of factories conforms to.\n *\n * Classes are found by name, so a single name cannot be registered twice for the same Base class.\n * Factories are registered by reference and this reference is expected to be valid through the life\n * of the program. should only occur in a single threaded\n * environment, which is guaranteed by the static instantiation mentioned above.\n *\n * Example lookup: BaseFactoryType *factory =\n * ret.reserve(factories().size());\n\n    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      if (factory || include_disabled) {\n        ret.push_back(factory_name);\n      }\n    }\n\n    std::sort(ret.begin(), ret.end());\n\n    return ret;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the current map of factory implementations.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factories() {\n    static auto* factories = new absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>;\n    return *factories;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the current map of vendor specific factory versions.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>&\n  versionedFactories() {\n    using VersionedFactoryMap =\n        absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, message type to a factory,\n   * including the deprecated configuration message types.\n   * Must be invoked after factory registration is completed.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factoriesByType() {\n    static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>* factories_by_type =\n        buildFactoriesByType().release();\n\n    return *factories_by_type;\n  }\n\n  static bool& allowDuplicates() {\n    static bool* allow_duplicates = new bool(false);\n    return *allow_duplicates;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * instead_value are used when passed name was deprecated.\n   */\n  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n    if (!result.second && !allowDuplicates()) {\n      ExceptionUtil::throwEnvoyException(\n          fmt::format(\"Double registration for name: '{}'\", factory.name()));\n    }\n\n are versioned\n   * independently of Envoy.\n   */\n  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n                              const envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion& corresponding\n   * factory pointer to null. If the factory is registered under multiple\n   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   */\n  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n      auto it = factories().find(name);\n      if (it != factories().end()) {\n        it->second = nullptr;\n        return true;\n      }\n      return false;\n    };\n\n    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n\n    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n        disable(deprecated_name);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n    return disable(canonicalName);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets a factory by name.   for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n      if (factory == nullptr) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      for (const auto& config_type : factory->configTypes()) {\n        ASSERT(!config_type.empty(), \"Extension config types can never be empty string\");\n\n        // Register config types in the mapping.\n        auto config_type, factory->name(),\n                                            it->second ? it->second->name() : \"\"));\n          it->second = nullptr;\n        } else {\n rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest() {\n    auto& mapping = factoriesByType();\n    auto updated_mapping = buildFactoriesByType();\n\n    // Copy the updated mapping over the old one.\n    mapping = *updated_mapping;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Replaces a factory by name.                        std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names = {}) {\n    using DeprecatedNamesVector = std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>>;\n\n    // If an existing prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name->configTypes(), factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') registered for tests\", factory.name(),\n                factory.configTypes());\n    }\n\n    factories().emplace(factory.name(), &factory);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(factory.name()) == &factory,\n                   \"test factory by-name deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, factory.name()));\n      }\n    }\n\n    rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest();\n\n    return [replacement = &factory, prev_by_name, It extends `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase` (line 203) and declares the pure virtual method `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` that returns an `absl::StatusOr<Http::FilterFactoryCb>`.\\n\\n**2. Factory Registry:**\\nThe `FactoryRegistry` template class (envoy/registry/registry.h:166) manages a static global registry of all factories indexed by name. Factories are registered at startup using the `RegisterFactory<T, Base>` template (envoy/registry/registry.h:507), which is instantiated through `REGISTER_FACTORY` or `LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY` macros. The registry stores pointers to factory instances in a static `absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>` (line 191).\\n\\n**3. Filter Chain Factory Interface:**\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:89) defines the `createFilterChain()` method, which is called when a new HTTP stream is created. It takes a `FilterChainManager` sink to receive filter instances.\\n\\n**4. HTTP Connection Manager Configuration:**\\nThe `HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory` (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h:53) is a network filter factory that creates HTTP connections. Its implementation (config.cc:274) calls the `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` constructor, which processes the list of configured HTTP filters and creates `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks during initialization.\\n\\n**5. Filter Chain Creation:**\\nThe `HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()` (config.h:141, config.cc:780) implements the `FilterChainFactory` interface. It calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc:17) with a pre-built list of filter factories.\\n\\nThe filter chain creation happens during server startup: each configured filter is looked up in the registry, its `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` method is called to produce a `FilterFactoryCb` (a std::function<void(FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&)>), and this callback is stored in a `FilterFactoriesList` (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h:51).\\n\\n**6. Per-Request Filter Instantiation:**\\nWhen a new HTTP request arrives, the filter chain creation is triggered per-request/per-stream:\\n\\n- The `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()` is called by the stream manager\\n- `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` iterates through stored `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks\\n- For each callback, `FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()` is called (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:697)\\n- The implementation in FilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:551) creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` and executes the stored callback with it\\n- The callback (created by the filter factory) calls `addStreamDecoderFilter()` or `addStreamEncoderFilter()` on the callbacks object (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:918, 924)\\n- These methods instantiate the actual filter instance and wrap it in `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` or `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter`, adding it to the stream's filter lists\\n\\n**7. Example Implementation:**\\nThe router filter (source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.h:18) shows the complete pattern: `RouterFilterConfig` extends `FactoryBase<ConfigProto>` and implements `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` (config.cc:14) which returns a lambda that captures the filter configuration and calls `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` with a new `Router::ProdFilter` instance. The factory is registered with `LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY()` (config.cc:32).\\n\\n**Key Design Points:**\\n- Configuration-time: Factories are looked up by name in the registry, and FilterFactoryCb callbacks are created and stored\\n- Request-time: Stored callbacks are executed to create actual filter instances for each request/stream\\n- The FilterFactoryCb std::function separates configuration (factories) from instantiation (callbacks), allowing efficient per-request filter creation\\n- Common factory base class (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h:63) provides template boilerplate for implementing filter factories\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1522,"cache_read_input_tokens":63681,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1522},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c5fff06b-3bb2-498f-83d9-3ef1ed1c4be4","uuid":"a145a65a-9fbe-4dae-9213-66742a2a48fc"}
